de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	The birth of a child that comes out with one hand extended.
I covient engignier a ramener la main:	It is necessary to engineer the return of the hand:
s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;	If it cannot be returned, then lift up the woman and go.
s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus .i. lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;	If she cannot walk, then lay her on a bed or couch with her legs spread apart.
puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit;	Then bring the muscle relaxant that I have mentioned before.
et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus .i. siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;	And if it does not bear a child [i.e., does not give birth], make her sit on a seat or chair, then study the method of returning the hand.
et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	And make her push according to natural form [i.e., give birth], and have her vomit, and command her to take hold of the child until it comes forth.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	Hold the baby by the neck and spread your hands apart, then turn your body towards the back of its mother.
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	The following text is a medieval medical treatise written in Old French, around the 12th-13th centuries.
et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;	And when it is even, put a strong mustard plaster of high altitude and oil on it, as we have said, then instruct him to move it little by little.
et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus .i. siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne; et la fai esternuer.	And when you have done that, make her sit on a seat and instruct her to grab it; then make her vomit.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	in the same way, treat all similarly
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	When it comes to swelling in this manner, seize the swelling with your nail until the moisture is voided;
et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;	and squeeze it on its face and neck, press the boil so that it is not retained, and let the boil die;
puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:	then insert the child, until you have placed it correctly, and command the woman to take it once.
adonques si istra legierement.	Therefore ease it gently.
de l’issue des gemelz	From the birth of twins   (In this context, "gemelz" refers to twins, as "gele" means a twin in Old French)
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent .iij. ou .iiij.; et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	Note that twins are born frequently and sometimes three or four; and this is not unusual, it happens often.   (The text uses Old French numerals "iii" for 3 and "iiij" for 4)
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	Two are unusual and do not live, if they can even be named;   (In this context, "dui" refers to a pair of twins who die at birth or shortly after)
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	I know this, that they should multiply, and are desired by the one who invents them, who is linked to filth.
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	And sometimes they issue in such a natural manner as the teeth of an animal, as we have said.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	And if they issue painfully, the cure is as we have said, and let the balm be subtle, and do it quickly and lightly whatever it does.
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	make it in such a way as it is worth remedying for health.
de plusors enfans	Of many children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris .i. ou .ij. ou .iij. ou .iiij. ou .v. ou .vj. ou .vij., ou plusors jusc’a .xv., et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious,	At times they are formed in the womb; one, two, three, four, five, six, seven or even more, up to fifteen, and they are all formed in the shape of a child according to the measurement of the noble sage,

si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	Follow as required.
de l’enfant mort	Of a dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	When treating the woman with a dead child or fetus, as I said in the division, and it does not come forth, and you are compelled to work by hand;    si faice selonc ceu qu'il covient.

et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	and this is the shape of the onyx:

et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	And if there remains no part, then put the interlocking device at a higher level and continue until it comes out completely.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement,	And if one hand comes before the other, and it cannot be returned due to the strain.

Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I marveled greatly because the belly has no bones.

dou ramener la marris a son leu	to bring back the marriage to its place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres; et a .ij. tornans as .ij. chiés des .ij. liiens.	Here follows the form of the pressor, to which one applies books; and at two turnings to the two heads of the two joints.

et enmi les .ij. liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	And between the two limbs there are two joints of the same bone, which are closed in one and the other, half a palm length or a little more;

Then work your hand with all the tools, just as you have done with the pliers equally, according to the quantity that you see to open the mouth of the swelling, until the patient allows it.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances; et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	These tools are all covered and have similar shapes; and when the physician has arranged them, he works more quickly, and higher for humans due to their size.

Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the afterbirth is retained during childbirth, you should instruct the patient to hold back her lochia (afterbirth fluid), and then make her vomit with emetics, and hold your hands at her mouth and nose.
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	If she jumps due to this, it is good.

toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu; puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris,	All these herbs, or some of them, should be cooked or boiled in water on the fire; then put a tube or a spout from the pot, and the other end into the mouth of the patient.

If it is to be pierced and reset, the pus will come out; however, if it does not heal properly, when it comes back, it will cause a bad smell in the stomach and head, making the patient sick.

de percier lou fondement	to drill the foundation
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born without having their foundations drilled, instead, it has been stopped up with some subtle substance;
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	Therefore, it is necessary to pierce the boil with a lance at its proper time, and not with a sharp spathulum, and to ensure that the lancing does not touch the ligament.

And if you doubt that it will reopen, place a leaden cannula over it (the boil), and leave it for several days, and remove it when the pus begins to move towards the rooms (of the body).

And sometimes this sudden swelling of wound or abscess occurs; it should be covered: whether it is healed, as we have said in the treatment of a poultice.
de la fistule dou fondement	of the fistula from the foundation
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des .ij. parties,	Fistulas that come from beneath the foundation are nodulation, and larger than those that come away from beneath it, or in the space of the two parts,

et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	And press your index finger or base into the fistula, and insert a fine awl of bone or iron into the fistula where there is no twisting.

saiches qu’elle ne perce mie; si te haste dou curer.	Know that it does not pierce [the skin]; hurry to treat it.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula has perforated up to the bladder or up to the conduit of urine, if it spouts urine and cannot heal with medicines.

s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	If it has no twisting and the pain is not around it, then it is a broken bone and cannot be healed with medicines or poultices.
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	And in these Persian blisters there is no remedy except labor, and the vain efforts of foolish people who meddle with it.

et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	and the aid one gives is as follows: if one heats the subtle cautery according to the width of the fistula, as previously stated;

si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	If the head of the fistula at its beginning, pushes ahead before the tent, and then the cautery afterwards, until it reaches the tip of the tent.

Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is restored, it becomes healed and does not return.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	If a fistula comes all the way up to the bottom, and is separated from the body, push your thumb or finger against the bottom, and check it.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre .ij. est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des .iii. manieres:	If you feel the temptation and there are two layers of fabric or sacking or charcoal, where it is about to pierce, there should be no remedy but a way of trust and hope through the administration of one of the three methods:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	or you cauterize it as we have said, or you press it to the bottom, or if it is inflamed, apply a poultice and cure it as we have described.
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	and do not go too deep, making sure to cover the foundation-holding material, and let the evacuation come out voluntarily.
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	Then heal, as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	By chance it may heal, or you remove that covering and clean it when it is cut from the foundation, whether by pressure or some other tool pointed;
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	then clean that charred material in the wound, as much as you can;
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement: si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	Then study to restore the wound, and to stop the fistula in the part beyond the foundation; it will be easier for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere: et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus,	And sometimes are fistulas in this manner: and it is when you press the tent (?) on the fistula, and it is where it touches the foundation below the skin above.
si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	and take a stentor's trumpet shaped in this way:
Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	and insert one thread twisted in two, and press the tent on the entire length of the thread into the fistula until it reaches the head (or top).
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it is pierced in the edge of the foundation inside, then extract the thread from that perforation, so that you press your thumb or foundation.
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les .ij. chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse .i. jor ou .ij.;	And draw the head through thread, and join the two shoulder-pieces together, and hold one against the other, and leave it for one or two days;
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	And do not tighten it at any time until the threads catch the cartilages that are between them and dislocate.
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	Then heal the wound until it is healed and sound.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not pierce through, make it pierce in all possible ways, if it is not too deep.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	It is not advisable to treat a dislocated joint by covering it tightly and then curing it while it is still unhealthy.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The shape of the spurred spine used to make a fistula is very sharp at one end and cuts through.
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	and not the other way round, because you should not cover what you should not cover, as you can see here:
des emorroydes	piles (hemorrhoids)
Emorrydes sont selonc ij. manieres: ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc,	Emorydes (emeroids) are of two types: they are within the foundation, like grains of resin, and there are small and large ones; and on the surface there is blood,  [or the translation can be] Emorydes come in two forms: either they are embedded within the foundations, similar to grains of resin, with some being small and others large; and on the surface there is bleeding.
et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement; mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor,	and one or more of them are dislodged from their foundation and from the base of the foundation; but those that are dislodged have little moisture.
et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	and at the same time or a small amount of clear yellow fluid or blood, and they take on the color of the body.
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	And the treatment of those who have it within the foundation, it is that you instruct the patient to stretch themselves towards going into rooms, until the foundations rise up and appear, and the sons understand.
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	Hurry, and you shall grasp it with pliers, or hold it with your nail, then strike it at its roots.
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a .i. drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	And if the scissors cannot hold them due to their moisture, take a linen cloth or cotton, or a piece of leather.
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	And pull [the dislocated joint] to your arms, then strike, and sprinkle hot powders over it instead of cautery;
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, puis les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	or cauterize [the wound] as the cautery chapter states, then heal it with other treatments until it heals;
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	and if the foundation cannot come out, then cauterize the patient with a hard and sharp clysteris to clean the affected area so that it can come out easily;
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	A sick person must prepare himself, and if his veins are forced from their foundation, it is an easy cure.
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	And it is that you grab them with your nail or tweezers, and strike them, then cure them as we have said, until they are healed and fear the incision by iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere: pren .i. fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les .ij. chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille,	It is necessary that you bring the stitching in this manner: take one twisted thread, put it into a needle, then pull the thread above and pierce the needle from the other side, and turn the two ends of the thread below the needle,
et si soit dou large; et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse .i. por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	And if it is wide; draw the thread, then knot it, and straighten the needle, and do the same with all the others, and leave one for draining excess blood;
puis met sus le fondement .i. drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	Then put on the foundation one moistened cloth in rose oil or pine resin, and place it on the wound, and instruct the patient to rest;
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And then leave it until it stops bleeding, and when it has stopped, you can treat it with salves and other remedies, until it heals;
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	The dry heat of the fire or foundation
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Often, there is dryness from fever in the intestines, and due to the natural constraint, when the sickness is old and medicine has no effect.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	You must cut the skin with a spatula or your nail so it does not get wet.    Car il se fait que le fiens deit mouvoir par ses movimens proprement, et si n’i puet adonques li sancs ne i coulent et li maladies ne se curent.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	Then let it heal as much as it should be.    Et quant il est sodez, purgez li fiens de sa feuillure, et fais que li sancs ne crescent pas en son intestine.
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	If it cannot heal, then start shaving again more forcefully than before, until it bleeds and is scratched;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then let it heal when it is healed.
dou fremit	toothache
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	Formicet is a small creature that crawls under the body and moves forward greatly;
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	And sometimes the thighbone breaks, and one feels it like death trembling, and it comes throughout the body, but more in the hands than elsewhere.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	The treatment is that you take a reed from an owl's feather or a strong vulture's feather and put the reed on the trembling, until the purple circles surround the trembling completely;
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	then turn your hand all around the reed until it covers the trembling completely, and push it in fully, and harden the trembling from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you see, do as with a cat's incision of honey or iron according to this form, and be subtle beneath and draw above.
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	Do not pierce, to keep the tooth, and press more; And if you see, cauterize the froth, as it is in the chapter of cautery.
de la forme dou clistere	of the form of the clyster   (enema)
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet; et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	Sometimes they make an enema of silver or arsenic, or melted beeswax or mallet; and sometimes they make these small and large instruments according to those for whom they are prepared.  (For the treatment of different ailments)
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Therefore, when treating children who are weak and painful, they are small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The shape of the cucurbit is both small and large, or the belly is tied in this manner:   (Note that "cucurbit" was incorrectly provided instead of "clistere".)
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez; et ait a l’un des costez .ij. pertus, et en l’autre .i.;	and it should have an opening where the belly is tied, as you see, and the eyes should be pierced within; and on one side there are two holes, and in the other one.  (Note that "costez" was incorrectly provided instead of "côtés".)
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus,	and the belly should be filled with medicine from a beast's bladder or parchment, and pierced all around with small holes,   (Note that "ventres" was incorrectly provided instead of "clistere".)
et ait entre chescun pertus .i. doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus .i. fil fort de fil crut tort en .x. ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	and place between each wound, namely a space, then push into these wounds, namely strong thread of twisted linen in ten or more, and bind the belly like a goat's.
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize; et c’est li forme dou cercle:	and when the medicine is within, tie it with a strong thread to the instrument in front, then cleanse (it). This is the shape of a circle.
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	And let the medicine not be too hot nor too cold, and anoint the head with oil or egg yolk, or similar thing, then insert it gently.
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses .ij. mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit,	Then the ministers press the patient's two hands together while he is fully visible, then remove the plaster, and wash the patient's legs in public.
et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet; et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	And if the medicine seems to work, squeeze as much as possible; and if it swells overnight, it is a greater help.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you plaster the patient with belly distention caused by gas, and the medicine appears to work quickly, continue until he is healed.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por .i. enfant;	And if the patient has hemorrhoids or abscesses, use a gentle plaster suitable for an infant.
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	and this is the form of the subtle suppository with which the skin should be stretched:
des plaies	in the treatment of wounds;
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies; or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	We have already said in the division the treatment for wounds; now we will tell you about the treatments and medicines for hands, according to the completion.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are diverse according to what they are made of, and according to the places where the wounds are made, and how they are made.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	The things by which wounds are made are by thrust of a spear, cut by sword and knife, or by lance or club or arrow, or similar things.
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	according to the parts of the body, such as wounds on the neck, or head, or chest, or belly, or liver, and similar members.
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	and I will tell you the cure for each wound, and I will begin with simple wounds of the head, because the memory will come in its chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans,	I say that when a simple wound or injury comes about where the bone is not broken, be careful if it is due to an arrow piercing or similar things, and the skin is entirely torn apart and the wound is large.
et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut: si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	and you doubt the lifting of the abscess: if it causes the wound to drain pus immediately, whether from the head or otherwise, let it drain against the injured part.
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	and let the patient avoid the accumulation of wine and heavy foods.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	And if it does not want to heal, reduce its flesh, and let it drink no wine, nor eat meat.
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	And put on the wound, if an abscess swells up there, only softened cotton in rose oil, or in stiptic wine.
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	And if there is no hot abscess, put on the wound if it is fresh with all its blood and not moved by the air, powder that I will say a little later.
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound has moved due to cold, put some ointments on until it heals.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	And if the wound is large like a sword and similar, and the lips cannot be brought together by sutures, bring them together by sewing, as I shall say for the abdominal wounds, with suturing.
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope; puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir,	If the wound is open to the bone, and pus-filled, and does not stay closed but only slightly, close it; then treat the wound with medicine, and restore hard flesh in place of skin.
et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	and command the patient to eat large foods such as heads (testes) and cooked wheat, also pulses, and similar things.
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	And if you find rot or putrefaction that does not reach the bone, cut off all the rotten part and pour boiling water on it, then treat it.
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	And if there is an artery in the wound or vein, from which it cannot be stopped without cutting, then you should cut the artery. If you find the artery dislocated, tie it with a thread.
et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	and if that does not help, cauterize [the wound].
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere: et est que tu mettes ens ceste poudre qui soude ainsois que li ars l’ait muee.	And if the wounds are small and simple, the cure is easy: it is that you put this powder on which hardens as soon as the arrows have moved [the wound].
Et li maniere de la poudre si est: pren encens une partie; sanc de dragon .ij. parties; chalz vive .iij. parties, et le poudre subtilment,	And the manner of the powder is: take one part of incense; two parts of dragon's blood; three parts of live coal, and grind it finely,   (Line 1)
et emple la plaie, et l’estraint forment, tant qu’elle s’aerse bien et se joigne a tout son sanc;	and apply the wound, and hold it open in shape, until it dries well and joins with all its blood;   (Line 2)
et puis la lie bien, et la laisse sens desliier, s’elle n’enfle; car on n’oste la madicine tant qu’ele soit sanee.	then tie it up well, and leave it to heal by itself if it does not swell; for one does not apply medicine until it is healed.   (Line 3)
Et aucune fois fait on ceu de chalz soulement, quant on n’ait l’encens ne lou sanc de dragon, mais que li ars n’ait muee la plaie.	And sometimes they do this with only chalk, when there is no incense nor dragon's blood, but the wound has not moved.
Et se li ars ait mueit la plaie, meismement en esteit, si n’i met om mie ceste poudre;	If the wound has moved, then do not use this powder at all.
mais met sus aucuns oignemens digestis, ou poulz de farine d’orge faites d’aigue et de miel, tant qu’ele giete bowe;	but place some digestible ointments or powder made from barley flour boiled in water and honey until it thickens.
puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then heal it with other treatments until it is healed.
Et se li brisure d’os vient avec la plaie, et elle est petite, si l’estrai as pinceures subtilz;	And if a bone fracture comes with the wound, and it is small, extract it with subtle forceps.
et je vos dirai ci aprés les brisures dou chief.	I will tell you next about the skull fractures.   (literal translation)
de la plaie dou col	of the neck wound    (literal translation)
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	If a wound comes to the neck and it is simple, there is no difference between it and one in the head, but if the nerve of the neck or the artery is cut.   (literal translation)
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire;	If it is nerves, there is no other remedy but to let them heal and not put anything binding, for it harms the nerves and causes them to retreat.
et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	And do not put anything cold on the wound, for the essence of the nerves is cold and their continuation with the brain, which is the highest member.
mais soit li medicine souez, si com chalz lavee en aigue douce, et mellee avec oile roset, et cucie lavee ausi en aigue douce,	but let the medicine be warm, such as salt washed in sweet water and mixed with rose oil, and cooked in warm water.
et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	and other stones of similar kind, and always moistened.
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound is large, bind it with strips, then let it heal until it becomes healthy.
Et se les plaies sont parfondes et ele est chevee et pleinne de bowe, si la perce ou plus bas leu;	If the wounds are deep and swollen with pus, pierce or cut them at a lower level.
et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est;	If the artery is cut and bleeding occurs, tie it off, clean it, and cauterize if necessary.
et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va,	If the spine of the throat is cut or the trachea is damaged, make sure that the food goes through it.   (The original text appears to be using "espinee" and "keurs" interchangeably to refer to the windpipe or trachea.)
si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel;	If the swelling is on the neck near the throat, do not touch the throat but reset it according to its natural shape.
et puis l’estrain avenanment, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le cure d’oignemens desechans tant qu’il soit sanez;	And then apply the treatment method and leave it for some days, then heal it with burning ointments until it is healed.
et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier;	And if the wound presses into the bone, cut it open.
et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse,	and if there are bone fragments, pull them out as you can, and leave the ones that you cannot remove until the wound festers.
et soit desevree et aligie li issue;	And let the joint be dislocated and aligned.
et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.	And if the wound is fresh, sprinkle powder on it as I have said.
Et s’il a en la plaie os et il i a fistule, si la cure ensi com j’ai dit en son chapistre.	If there is bone in the wound and a fistula, treat it as I have said in its chapter.
de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	of the wound from a lance or knife
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne: saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	If it is a sword or dagger wound, and the wound is deep, check if vapors rise from the wound as the patient breathes; then know that the wound is fatal.
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont,	and if it is not deep, and the wound is fresh with all its blood, do not put powder on it immediately nor bind it for fear of causing bleeding.
et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	return to the patient's heart, and cut open the sick person;
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie .ij. fois le jor;	but apply an attractive ointment, and let it rest for two times the hour.
et se tu n’as oignement, si met en la plaie viel coton por succier fuers la moistor,	and if you don't have ointment, place old cotton in the wound to absorb moisture.
et fai dormir le malaide sus la plaie .iij. jors, ou .iiij., ou plusors;	make the patient rest above the wound for three days or four, or more.
si n’i venra mie spasme, ne tremor male de cuer n’es traingnemens d’alainne;	if no convulsion or bad trembling of the heart occurs, do not bind with linseed.
et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	And when you see good positions, know that the wound is healed.
Cure la donques de tentes et d’autres cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Perform the cure then from tents and other treatments, as long as he is healthy.
et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule; si la cure si com on doit.	If it cannot be cured, and it opens up, then know that there is a fistula; if so, treat it as appropriate.
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	If the wound is from a sword or knife cut, and it is simple (i.e., not complex), whether on the front or back, treat the part that is in front of it.  \]
s’elle est grans, de cousture; et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	If it is large, sew (it); if it is small, powder (it); and if it is pressed into the bone, and has pieces attached to it, whether it be a wound, and the flesh is torn away, pull it apart if it is detached;
et s’il ne sont desevrez, si laisse porrir la plaie, si aligera li estractions;	and if they are not torn away, let the wound drain, align the extraction.
et des autres plaies as autres membres est li jugemens si com nos avons dit.	And for other wounds on various limbs, the judgments are as we have said.
dou derrompement dou ventre	The displacement of the abdomen
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	The displacements of the abdomen are large, medium, and small.
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	From a large wound, the intestines sometimes protrude, or the bowels of the intestines, due to which the introduction of anything inside it.
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans,	and the stitching is more difficult, and sometimes a small wound is worse than a large one,
por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	Because it is better to return the intestines more gradually, if not put them back bit by bit.
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes,	As they swell quickly when feeling cold, therefore they should be returned more gradually.
et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres .ij.	and because it is better to treat the middle wound, because it is easier to reset the intestines in their place than others.
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc .iiij. manieres:	And know that the opening of the belly can be according to four methods:
les .ij. costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre,	The two common sutures happen in the abdominal suture.
et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et .ij. autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	and the sutures of other wounds on the body and two other specific sutures are common for other wounds.
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	Moreover, they are more suitable with the abdominal suture, and I will explain one of them and declare it.
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer,	I say that when the wound is small, and anything from the intestine protrudes,
et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des .ij. manieres:	And great care is needed when resetting, this can be done by one of the two ways:
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit,	or by the smallness of the wound, as we have said,
ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	or because the intestines are swollen due to cold.
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	And when it is cold, warm it in such a way:
moillie une esponge ou .i. mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement,	Soak a sponge or a linen cloth only in cold water.
ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique,	cook it in boiling water with juniper berries and spikes.
et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	remove the intestines while it is inflated.
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	and sometimes make wine pressings, and it is matured until it swells to open.
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites,	And when you see the swelling separate, if you want to treat the intestines with either hot or cold and harmful foods,
car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	for this will close the entrance to almost nothing;
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	and if it cannot enter, make a small wound with the instrument used for removing hemorrhoids;
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille,	and the first remedy is a poultice that cuts;
que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	We should not cut it without great necessity.
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	and this is the instrument for splitting:
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	if you cut within the curve and bend not, and look here at the shape.
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer,	When the wound is enlarged, and the intestines burst through,
si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre,	If you reset [it] according to its natural form in its proper place,
se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	If you have the power, because it is worth making the effort.
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre,	When the wound is wide and it is in the part below the stomach,
si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos,	If you should make the patient lie on his back,
et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	And raise his legs higher than his head;
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre,	And if it is in the part beneath the abdomen,
si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz,	lift up the head and the foot higher than the parts below;
et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des .ij. parties	and similarly if the hernia is in one of the two parts of the abdomen
si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	If the part broken is higher than the other;
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	and such should be administered for large and small wounds.
Es plaies petites met ceu que t’est apparilliet,	In small wounds, use what is appropriate;
puis aies entre tes mains .i. ministre pitous ki teigne toute la routure a sa main,	then have between your hands a minister who knows the entire route of the wound with his hand,
et assemble les levres;	And press the lips;
et c’est la maniere commune de costures,	And this is the common way of suturing.
et est que tu preignes une aguille ou plusors, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce de la plaie,	And take a needle or more as per the width of the wound.
puis laisse des le chief de la plaie .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une aguille ou il ait .i. boin fil fort;	Leave one finger's width from the edge of the wound and insert a needle with a single strong thread.
et perce les .ij. chiés dou cuir avec les .ij. chiés dou siphac,	and pierce the two shoulders with the two chisels of the syphac,
qui est desoz le cuir dedens, tant que tu la faices percier de celle partie,	which is beneath the skin inside, as long as you make it pierce from that part,
et assemble les .ij. chief dou siphac les .iiij. ensamble;	and put together the two shoulders of the syphac in four pieces;
puis l’estrain d’un fil double entor l’aguille de .ij. pars,	then pull a double thread around the awl of two parts,
puis assemble les .ij. chiés de la plaie avenanment,	Then assemble the two heads of the wound together.
et puis laisse .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une autre aguille;	and then leave one finger's width of space, and insert another needle.
puis la lie dou fil si com tu as fait la premiere aguille,	then tie the thread as you did with the first needle,
et ne cesser de ceu faire selonc ceu que tu as mestier des aguilles,	and do not stop doing this according to your need for the needles.
tant que toute li plaie soit restrainte;	Until the whole wound is bound up;
et soient les aguilles moienes, entre subtilz et grosses,	and the needles be moderate, neither too thin nor thick,
car les aguilles subtilz copent toute la char, et les trop grosses si ne pueent mie bien entrer:	for fine needles penetrate the entire skin, and thick ones cannot enter well:
por ceu covient qu’elles soient moienes;	Because they should be reduced (or set back in place).
et ne covient mie bouter les aguilles trop au defuer de la char et dou cuir,	and it is not good to push the needles too far into the flesh and skin,
k’elles ne copent et oevrent la plaie devant la soudure;	so that they do not open and widen the wound before the healing.
et puis cope les chiés des aguilles, qu’elles ne blecent lou malaide au dormir,	Then place the needles on the joints so they do not hurt the patient while sleeping,
et i met tentes ou drapelz au chiés des aguilles por mues tenir,	And he sets needles or bandages on the head of the arrows to hold them in place.
et les laisse tant que li plaie soit soudee;	And let it remain until the wound is healed.
et ceste maniere de costure as aguilles est plus covenauble en petites plaies,	This method of stitching with needles is more suitable for small wounds,
car il i soffist une aguille ou .ij.	because it pierces an arrow or two.
Li seconde costure si est commune,	The second suture is common.
et est que tu assemble les .ij. chiés dou cuir et les .ij. chiés dou syfac ensamble a une aguille ou il ait .i. fort fil moien;	and that you join the two shoulder blades with the two ribs together with a needle having one strong, medium-sized thread;
et quant tu avras perciez ces chiez toz .iiij. ensamble,	and when you have pierced these four together,
si ramoinne l’aguille a la partie ou tu as encomenciet, en la maniere c’on cout les dras;	if you remove the needle from the part where you began, in the manner that one sews a dress;
et met d’espaice entre chescune costure la grossece d’un menor doi;	And put space between each stitch the thickness of a hen's egg.
ceste costure sevent li home,	this stitch shall be for the man.
et je cousi une plaie c’uns hons avoit ou ventre,	and I sew a wound that a man had in his belly,
qui estoit navrez d’un coutel,	who was wounded by a knife,
et estoit li plaie plus d’une palme de grant,	and the wound was more than one palm in length,
et issoit des intestines bien .ij. palmes de grant,	and extended from the intestines two palms in length,
et estoit li plaie enmi le ventre.	and was in the abdomen.
Je li ramenai l’intestine puis k’il ot esteit .xxiiij. houres fuer,	I returned his intestines as it had been 24 hours ago.
et fut li plaie soudee jusc’a .xv. jors, et le curai, et fut sanez.	and the wound healed in 15 days, and it was cured, and became healthy.
Et li mire l’avoient jugiet qu’il morroit, et ce fut miracle;	And they had judged that he would die, and it was a miracle;
et ne le curai mie d’oignement, car je estoie en .i. leu ou on n’en trovoit point, ne nule medicines;	and I did not cure him with medicine, because I was in one place where none could be found, nor any remedies;
et metoie sens plus sus la plaie coton viel .ij. fois le jor, et le lavoie d’aigue de miel tant qu’il fut sanez.	And put cotton wool over the wound several times a day, and wash it with water of honey until it is clean.
Or vos dirai les .ij. propres manieres de cousture:	I will tell you the two proper ways of sewing:
pren l’aguille, et la boute des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens;	Take the needle, and thread it from the outside to the inside part.
quant elle a perciet le keur de droit en droit, si lai le chief dou siphac ou cousteit ou tu as bouteit l’aguille,	When the needle has pierced through straight in straight, place the knot at the end where you inserted the needle.
et la fai percier d’autre part des la partie dedens jusc’a celi defuer;	And pierce it through from the inside part until it comes out there.
et li entendemens de ceste costure si est que tu cous ausi com li peletier font les pelz,	and understand that you sew in this manner as a tailor makes fur pelts,
et que tu laisses une fois le syfac d’une part, et le reprent d’autre, tant que li costure soit toute acomplie.	and leave the syringe from one side at a time, and refill it with the other, until the stitching is completely finished.
Li seconde maniere de costure, que Galiens dist proprement,	The second method of stitching, which Galen calls specifically,
si est si com aucun font, qui assemblent les .ij. parties ensamble naturelment,	is like what anyone who joins two parts together naturally,
et apploient l’un des chief dou syfac a l’autre chief, en teil maniere:	and apply one end of the thread to the other end in this manner:
fiche une aguille ou chief dou mirach prochiene, et fai percier celui leu soulement,	thread a needle or end of the silk nearest to that point, and pierce only that place,
et laisse les .ij. chiés dou syfac;	And let the two shoulders be still.
puis torne l’aguille, et la fai percier des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens,	then turn the needle and make it pierce from the outer part to within that (the inner) part.
as .ij. chiés dou syfac;	as the two shoulders are still.
puis fai percier l’un et l’autre des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, en .ij. autres chiés dou mirach que sont on l’autre costeit;	then pierce one and the other from the outer part to within that (the inner) part, in two other shoulders opposite each other.
et c’est li muedre maniere de costure et li plus commune.	And this is the moistened manner of stitching, and it is the most common.
Galiens si dist ceste parolle, et aucun le tesmoignent,	Galen said this word, and no one can deny it,
c’on doit coudre le ventre a .ij. aguilles, ou il ait fil en chescune;	One must sew the stomach with two needles, where there is thread in each.
et doit on bouter l’une aguille d’une part, et l’autre d’autre, en la maniere de ces qui cousent corroies;	And one needle must be thrust from one side, and another from the other, in the manner of those who sew leather.
et saiches que quant li routure est enmi lou ventre,	Know that when the hernia is inside the abdomen,
si est li cousture plus griez que des autres leus dou ventre.	the repair is more difficult than in other parts of the abdomen.
Li jugemens de la plaie si est telz com li jugemens des autres plaies:	The measurements for the wound are similar to those for other wounds:
et est que quant tu trueves la plaie fresche a tout son sanc, ainsois que li ars l’ait muee,	And it is when you find the fresh wound full of blood, just as the arrow has moved it.
si remet arer l’intestine, et lou cout; puis met sus la poudre enjanrant char,	Then place the intestine back in its place, and sew it up; then put powder on the wound to heal it.
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucun oignement que soit present, tant que li plaie bowe;	If the arrow has moved it, then place any salve that is present on the wound until it heals.
et chicent li fil, et soient soudez li sifac, et li mirach;	and close the flesh, and sew the edges together with the thread, and apply pressure to stop the bleeding.
puis cure la plaie si com les autres, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then treat the wound as others, when it is healthy.
et se tu n’as medicines, si met sus, tantost qu’ele comance a giter bowe, coton viel,	And if you have no medicine, put on it immediately when it begins to emit pus, old cotton.
et le remue .ij. fois le jor tant k’il soit sanez.	And stir it twice a day until it is healthy.
Car tu n’as mestier d’autre medicine en plusors dispositions cant les plaies sont simples;	You have no need for any other medicine when simple wounds occur in multiple positions.
et se tu doutes que li plaie ne faice communiteit as membres principelz,	and if you doubt that the wound will communicate with the principal members,
si covient ke tu moilles lainne legiere en oile de tempree chalor, ou en oile roset,	you must moistened light linen with warm oil or rose oil,
et la met entor les angres, et desoz les asselles;	And place it among the bones, beneath the joints;
et s’il sent dolor ou porriture en bouelz, et maintes fois avient,	And if there is pain or rottenness in the belly, and it happens many times,
si les clisterize de vin noir tede, et meismement se li porriture vient jusc’a l’intestine;	if the cleansing with black wine is heated, and particularly when the rottenness comes to the intestine;
et le perce dedens, et saiches que quant c’est li gros intestines, si est plus legier a saner que li petis.	And piercing within, know that when it is the large intestines, it is easier to heal than the small ones.
Li intestine qui est apelez «jeun» ne puet saner quant il est navrez,	The intestine called "jeun" cannot heal when it is pierced.
et c’est por la planteit des voinnes que i sont, et por la subtiliteit de tout le cors, et l’aprochement de sa nature des ners.	and it is because of the planting of veins in them, and the subtlety of the entire body, and the closeness of its nature to nerves.
Et si li zirbe saut de la plaie, si le remet arrier ausi com l’intestine, tandis qu’il est fres;	And if the suture jumps from the wound, put it back as the intestine, while it is still fresh;
et s’il est vielz et devenus vers ou noir, si covient que tu lies le leu qui est noir, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne,	And if it becomes old and turns black, you must cauterize the black spot so that blood does not flow from it.
car il i a voinnes et arteres;	For there are veins and arteries;
puis cope ceu qui est entre le liien,	then strike what is between the ligament,
et met les .ij. chiés pendans des la partie desoz la plaie jusque defuer por aligier l’estraction quant li zirbes chiet, et li plaie bowe.	and hang the two heads on the part under the wound to straighten the extraction when the arrows fall out, and the wound opens.
de la routure dou boueil	Of the rupture of the eyeball
Quant li intestine est rons, et li plaie est petite,	When the entrails are torn, and the wound is small,
si la puet on restorer en aucuns homes,	it can be restored in some men,
por ceu que je vis que uns hons fut navrez ou ventre d’une lance;	because I have seen that a man was pierced or wounded by a lance;
et estoit li plaie au destre de l’estomac,	And the wound was on the right side of the stomach,
et fut envillie et devint fistule, et en issoit li egestion et li ventositez;	and it became inflamed and turned into a fistula, and there were excretions and flatulence in it;
je i mis cure selonc ceu que je poi, et ne cessai de subtilier tant qu’il fut sanez, et li leus soudez.	I treated it according to what I knew, and did not stop the application until it was healed, and the wounds were sealed.
Et quant je le vis souder, je doutai que li malaides n’eust mal en son ventre;	And when I saw that the wound was healed, I feared that the patient might have something wrong in his stomach;
et il n’i ot point de mal, mais demora en millors dispositions, et menjans et bevans;	And there was no ill, but it remained in better positions, and ate and drank;
et dirent aucun experimentors que quant il a petite plaie en l’intestine, qu’il doit estre liiez en teil maniere:	and said some experimenters that when there is a small wound in the intestines, it should be tied in this way:
pren fremis a grans testes, puis assemble les levres de la plaie,	take firm grips with large hands, then gather together the lips of the wound,
et quant li fremis ait overte la bouche, si la met sus les .ij. levres,	and when the hand has opened the mouth, place it on the two lips (or: lips of the wound),
si qu’elle estraigne sa bouche sus;	if it opens its mouth up;
et puis li cope la teste, et ce se tient si qu’il ne puet desliier,	and then strike the head, and hold it so that it cannot dislocate.
puis met .i. autre fremit aprés en celle maniere que devant, tant que li plaie soit toute porprise;	then put another blow in the same way as before, until the wound is completely seized;
et cout la plaie.	and stitch up the wound.
Cil chief si s’aerdent en l’intestine, et ne vient nulle nuisance au malaide,	If the head swells in the intestines, it causes no harm to the patient.
et se puet on liier l’intestine d’un fil subtil qui est copez de l’intestine d’une beste,	and a thin string made from the intestine of an animal can be used to tie the intestines.
en teil maniere:	in this manner:
pren le chief de cest fil d’intestine que soit mout descharnez,	Take the head of this intestinal thread that is very thin.
et puis lie au chief de cest fil .i. fil de lin subtil tort,	and then tie it to the head of this thin thread (or fine cord) made from flax.
puis boute le fil en l’aguille, et en cout l’intestine, et le ramoinne en la routure;	then put the thread in a needle, sew the intestine, and tie it at the opening.
et ceste maniere de costure de fremis nen est fuers que selonc la voie de fiance et d’esperance;	and this way of sewing up hernias is not without its risks and uncertainties;
et se li plaie est grans et large, meismement quant elle est en l’un des grailes intestines, si n’i a engien ne santeit, fuer que subtiliteit.	And if the wound is large and wide, especially when it is in one of the great intestines, there is no remedy nor health, unless through subtlety.
de fistule ou qu’ele soit	of fistula or that it be
Saiches que toute plaie ou aposteme, quant il enveillist, si est apelee universement «fistule»,	Know that every wound or abscess, when it heals, is universally called "fistula,"
et meismement quant elle est chevee et rent bowe.	and especially when it is closed and swollen.
Et fistule est selonc la verteit nodation fautree dure et blainche, ou on ne sent dolor,	And a fistula is according to the truth, formed by hard and white knot, where no pain is felt.
et est ausi chevee com li penne d’un oiseil;	and it is closed like the feather of a bird;
et aucune fois en saut clere bowe, et autre fois espesse;	and sometimes it clears up in a clear jump, and other times it thickens.
aucune fois poc, et autre fois assez;	sometimes it decreases, and other times it increases.
et je en ai jai parleit en la division des plaies, que toute plaie que n’est sanee, et il n’i a char,	And I have spoken about it in the section on wounds, that every wound which is not healed, there is no flesh,
ce n’est fuers que par une des .viiij. causes:	this is only due to one of the eight causes:
c’est a savoir, par la petitece dou sanc ou cors;	it is to know, by the small amount of blood or body heat;
ou por sa malice;	or by its mischief,
ou por ceu qu’il i a char dure dedens, et sus les levres, que n’i laisse naistre char;	Because there is hard flesh within, under the skin, do not let it grow.
ou il i a trop de bowe;	If there is too much pus.
ou li leus est porris, et li matiere est de male qualiteit;	When the loin (lower abdomen) is swollen, and the substance is of bad quality.
ou li medicine n’est mie bone en la cure;	If the medicine is not good in the treatment.
ou por ceu que li corruption est maniere de pestilence;	For because corruption is a kind of pestilence;
ou por la proprieteit en la region est tardive li digestion, et tarde li santeit, et enflee par nature;	For the property in the region causes slow digestion, and the health delays, and it melts naturally on its own.
ou il i a voinnes ou os:	There are veins or bones;
et j’ai ja mostreit toutes ces causes, et les signes, et les cures de medicines en la division.	And I have already shown all these causes, and the signs, and the treatments of medicines in the division.
Or covient que je te faice a savoir la cure de fistule qui est faite par oevre de mains.	Therefore it is necessary that I tell you the treatment for fistula which is done by handwork.
Saiches que fistule avient en tous membres dou cors;	Know that fistula occurs in all members of the body;
car il i a fistules que vienent as grans voines, et as arteres, et as ners,	because there are fistulas that come from large veins, arteries, and nerves.
ou au syfac, ou a l’intestine, ou a la vessie, ou a aucunes des costes,	or the intestines, or the bladder, or the kidneys, or any of the ribs,
ou a l’espinee dou dos, ou a aucune jointe des mains ou des piez;	or to the spine in the back, or any joint in the hands or feet;
et si a teil que vient a la proprieteit dou membre principeil, et as semblans leus.	and if it is such that it affects the principle part of the limb, and similar things.
Et toutes les fistules que sont de ceste maniere sont de grief sanation, et n’i a fors que labour, et ignorance;	And all the fistulas of this kind are difficult to cure, and there is only labor and ignorance involved.
et se il i a aucune fistule que ne veigne mie jusc’a leu que j’ai dit, et tu as fiance de la cure,	And if there is no fistula that does not reach the level I have said, and you have faith in the cure,
et tu la vues conoistre, si pren une tente d’arain ou de fer, se li fistule est droite, si la quier;	and you see it understood, if you take a tent of beeswax or iron, if the fistula is straight, press it;
et se li fistule est torte, si la cerche d’une subtil tente de plonc,	and if the fistula is twisted, search for a subtle tent of lead,
car li plons se ploie mues entor la tortuositeit;	because lead bends with twisting.
et se li fistule a mains pertus et tu ne la pues mie bien cerchier par tentes,	And if the fistula at the hands is pierced and you cannot find it well by probing.
si la clisterize par l’un des pertus,	if the fistula through one of the wounds,
car la moistors si cort d’un pertus a autre, et la mundifie;	because moisture is so short from one wound to another and cleans it.
puis la quier saigement a ton pooir, que tu conoisses s’il i a os ou nerf, et est chevee em parfont,	then seek it cauterily within your power, that you know if there is bone or nerve and it has reached fully.
et demande bien au malaide de la dolor qu’il sent au presser de ta main, et le leu ou il la sent;	And ask the patient well about the pain they feel at your touch, and where they feel it.
et quant tu savras vraiement le leu ou elle est, et s’elle est loing de jointure, ou de nerf, ou d’artere ou de voine,	And when you truly know the place where it is, and if it is far from a joint, or nerve, or artery or vein.
ou en aucuns des leus que je t’ai dit, si la cope selonc ceu que je t’ai dit,	Or in any of the places that I have told you, as I have said, if it is broken as I have told you.
et oste fuer la fautreure et les chars corrumpues que sont dedens;	and cut open the fracture and the rotten bones that are inside.
et puis la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee,	And then the treatment until it heals,
et se li fistule est bien parfonde de droit endroit, si covient que tu copes em parfont, tant com tu pues,	If the fistula is well penetrated directly, you must cut through completely, as much as you can,
puis i met tentes moillies en medicine ague, et les boute jusc’au chief de la fistule,	Then put dampened plasters with strong medicine inside it, and push them up to the end of the fistula,
tant que li medicine corrode la superfluiteit qui est demoree au fons;	until the medicine corrodes the excess that remains at the bottom.
et puis i met oignemens enjanrans sainne char, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And then apply salve-like ointments to healthy skin, as long as it is clean.
et s’il n’est sanez par ceu, si le cauterize si com nos avons dit,	and if it is not clean in this way, cauterize it as we have said,
et se li os est corrompus de la fistule, si le cope.	And if the bone is rotten due to a fistula, cut it off.
Se voinne ou ners ne te greve ou membres principelz, si com nos avons dit;	If a vein or nerves do not obstruct or principal members, as we have said;
et se li os est descovers, et il i a corruption et noiror, si lou reis tant que li corruption soit toute ostee,	and if the bone is exposed, and there is corruption and blackness, let it heal until all the corruption is removed,
puis le cure de choses enjanrans char tant qu’il soit sanez;	then cure it with things that are healing and clean until it is healed;
et s’il n’est sanez, et rent bowe si com devant,	If it is not healed, return to what was mentioned before,
saiches que tu n’es mie alez jusc’a font:	Know that you are not going as far as the fountain:
si descuevre et quier tant que tu soies au fons,	ung peregrin en la terre de Grescoigne.
et oste toute la corruption, puis restore le leu;	and remove all corruption, then restore its place;
et s’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	if he is thus sound, that's good.
Se ceu non, saiches que la corruption est trop en parfont, que tu n’i pues avenir;	If not (the shoulder), know that the corruption is too advanced, that you cannot reach it.
si n’i a autre engien que dou lassier a nature;	if there is no other means but to let it heal by itself.
et s’il i a i petit os corrumput, et tu le pues traire as tenailles,	and if there is a small bone corruption, and you can extract it with pliers.
si l’estrai a .i. estrument covenauble a ceu,	if it can be extracted with one instrument.
et s’il i a maint os, si les trai trestoz, ne n’en laissier nes un;	And if there are many bones, draw them all out, do not leave any of them.
et se li moistor te fait contraire, et il n’i a error ne paour,	and if the moisture opposes you, and there is no mistake or fear,
si cope et moistor et char, et delivre les os.	if flesh and moisture and cartilage block the bones, free the bones.
Et se tu ne les pues oster a une houre, si met sus la plaie chose enjanrant porriture,	And if you cannot remove them within an hour, put on the wound something to promote decay (poultice)
et laisse tant que li leus soit porris entor les os,	And let the ligaments grow around the bones,
et adonc si avront plus legierement les os;	then they will have more easily movable bones;
et se c’est uns grans os, si com de jambe ou de cuisse,	and if it is a large bone like the leg or thigh,
si reis tant soulement la corruption tant que li noiror soit toute ostee,	then clean only the rottenness so that all the blackness is removed,
puis restoure la plaie;	Then restore the wound;
et s’il en i a grant partie dou corrumput, et vient jusc’a mole de l’os;	and if there is a large part corrupt and comes to the bone marrow;
si le covient soier et coper tout jusc’a la corruption, et puis le cure tant qu’il soit soudez;	it must be cut off and covered up to the corruption, and then heal until it is healed;
et je te dirai d’une fistule qui avint .i. home en sa jambe,	and I will tell you of a fistula that happened in a man's leg,
si que tu i preignes exemple et aide en ton ovraige.	If you take an example and aid in your work.
Il fut .i. jovencelz entor .xxx. ans, qui ot une dolor en sa jambe d’une cause que vint dedens le cors,	There was a young man of about thirty years old who had pain in his leg due to something coming from within the body.
tant que les matieres vinrent a la jambe, et fut enflee d’un gros aposteme, et n’ot point de cause defuer por ovrir;	and matter came to the leg, and a large abscess broke out that could not be opened up further.
mais li mire par lor folie ovrerent tant sus que li apostemes ovri,	but the monks, out of their foolishness, opened up the abscesses too much,
et en corroient mout de matieres, et devint fistule, et i vint mout de pertus que tuit gitoient bowe et moistor dou cors;	And it becomes filled with a lot of matter, and it turns into an abscess, and much pus flows from it that all runs downwards with moisture from the body.
et maint mire i mirent cure entor .ij. ans, et n’i ot nul saige en l’art de mains,	And many people put various cures around it for two years, and there was no skilled healer among them in the art of hands.
tant que je i fui apelez, et vi sa jambe et les medicines dont on le curoit,	As long as I was present, I saw his leg and the medications they used to treat him,
et ceu que corroit par les pertus a grant cors;	And those who run through the wounds with great haste;
et devenoit rouges li cors dou jouvenceil, et avoit color citrine.	And the youth's body becomes red, and had a citron-colored complexion.
Je boutai une tente en l’un de ces pertus, et puis cerchai toz les pertus,	I pitched a tent at one of these wounds, and then searched all the wounds,
et trovai que li uns venoit encontre l’autre de toutes les parties de la jambe.	And I found that one bone comes against another from all parts of the leg.
Je me hastai donques, et copai en l’un des pertus tant que je descovri une partie de l’os,	I then, took in one wound as far as I discovered a part of the bone,
et le trovai corrumput et perciet, et venoit li corruption jusc’a l’os dedens;	and I found it rotten and pierced through, and the rot came up to the bone within;
je soiai ceu qui m’aparissoit de l’os corrumput, et cuidai qu’il n’i eust autre corruption, fuer que celi que je ostai;	I was the one who seemed to see the rotten bone, and thought that there was no other rot except for what I left.
et comensai a restourer la plaie de medicines sodans par lonc tens, et ne pot souder;	And it began to heal the wound with salty medicine for a long time, but could not be closed.
et puis rencomensai, et descovri l’os si com devant,	Then it was reinforced, and discovered the bone as before,
et trovai la corruption continuee en l’os, et la soiai, et puis l’ostai, et me penai de souder le leu;	and found the continuous corruption in the bone, cut it out, left it open and tried to close the wound.
mais je ne pou tant que je copai entor une palme de l’os, et le traï fuer a tout son mole,	but I could not as I wrapped around a palm of the bone, and pulled it off completely,
puis le restourai de medicines; et il fut sanez et soudez hastanment,	Then restore it with medicines; it healed and hardened quickly.
et ne covint plus rencomencier l’ovraige fors por la foibleté dou malaide, qui ne pooit soffrir,	and it should not be necessary to start the work again except due to the weakness of the patient who could not endure.
et por la paour de mort que je avoie de lui.	and because of the fear of death that I had for him.
Car por l’evacuation sanglotoit sovent, mais il fut sanez entierement,	Because it often bled from evacuation, but he was entirely healed.
et nasquit en leu de l’os une char dure, et fut de bone disposition et n’ot point de nuisement ne de contraire dou tout en tout, ne a l’aleir ne a venir.	And a hard cartilage is born in the place of the bone, and it has good alignment and no harm or contrary to anything, neither at the side nor at the coming.
Et se li os est brisiez en aucun leu dou cors, si le covient soier en ceste maniere:	And if the bone is broken in any part of the body, it must be done in this manner:
pren .i. liien, et l’estrain au chief de l’os qui apert,	Take a ligature and tighten it at the opening of the broken bone.
et comande aucun k’il l’estende en haut;	Command anyone to stretch it upwards;
et met .i. autre lien de lainne plus gros dou premier liien, et le lie sus la char qui est desor l’os,	and put another thread of coarse linen larger than the first one, and tie it above the cartilage that is detached from the bone,
et estent le chief, si que tu traies la char corrumpue au desoz,	stretch the head so you pull out the corrupted cartilage underneath,
et descuevre la char sus le leu ou tu vues soier, que li soie ne blece la char;	uncover the cartilage on the correct place where you want to be, so that the skin does not cut the cartilage;
et met .i. tison ou une tauble desoz l’os por mues coper la char corrumpue;	And put, either a splint or a table beneath the bone to cover the corrupt flesh;
et covient tant soier com on puet veoir et sentir la corruption, et soier ancor autre fois.	And it is necessary that it be as small as possible, and to see and feel the corruption, and to be more often.
Et se li os est corrumpus, et n’apert mie, et li corruptions est en mileu ou en une partie,	And if the bone is corrupt and does not open, and the corruption is in the middle or a part of it,
si descuevre la char toute; puis met .i. tison desoz,	if you uncover the entire flesh; then place a splint under it,
et puis soie des l’une partie a l’autre la corruption, et soit li soieure dou lonc de la corruption .i. poc, si com nos avons dit;	And let there be from one part to another the corruption, and let the length of the corruption be a span (or 9 inches), as we have said;
et se li corruptions est en la jointure, si cope la jointure corrumpue, et soie l’os ou elle contient de l’autre part;	If the corruption is in a joint, then strike the corrupt joint, and let the bone on the other side be exposed;
et se li corruptions est en la continuation des .ij. jointes, si n’i a autre angien que dou coper;	And if the corruption is in the continuation of two joints, then there is no remedy but to cover it up;
et se li corruptions est ou poignil de la main, ou ou poignil dou piet, si est mout fort celle chose,	If the corruption is at the wrist (of the hand) or ankle, it is a very difficult thing,
mais toutevoie il covient que tu enquieres celle corrosion, coment elle t’apert;	But always it is necessary that you inquire about that corrosion, how it opens up;
et la mundifie en toutes les manieres que tu pues, mais que li voine ou li nerf ne te faicent contraire;	and clean it in every way that you can, but let the vein or nerve not hinder you;
et saiches que li incisoire et les soies por coper ces os sont maintes, selonc l’assise des os et l’aparance d’ous,	And know that the saw and files for cutting these bones are many, according to the position of the bone and its appearance,
et lor grossece et lor subtiliteit, et lor grandor et lor petitece, et lor duresce;	And their thickness and fineness, and their greatness and smallness, and their hardness;
et por ceu covient il apareillier a chescune semblance d’ovraige son estrument;	and for this reason, the instrument must be prepared according to each kind of work.
et saiches que l’uevre te moustrera l’estrument dont tu avras mestier, selonc la conissance de cest art,	And know that the work will show you the tool needed, according to the knowledge of this art,
et le tesmoignaige des manieres des maladies;	and the testimony of the signs of diseases.
si porpense l’estrument dont tu as mestier selonc ceu qu’il le covient.	If one considers the tool required for what is necessary according to this.
dou feu	of fire
Li chiés porrissent ou par cause dedens, ou par cause defuer;	The head may dislocate either due to internal or external causes;
et quant tu avras medicinee celle corrosion par la cure des medicines, et il ne profitent mie,	and when you have treated that with corrosive medicine and it does not help at all,
si covient coper celui membre jusques au leu ou li corrosion vient,	It is necessary to cover that member up to the level where the corruption comes.
si que li malaides eschaipe par ceu de la mort, ou par la malice, qui est plus grans, de la defaute dou membre;	If the patient escapes death by this means or by some greater evil, which is lack of a member,
et li signes si est que li membres devient noir, si qu’il semble qu’il soit ars dou feu,	and the signs are that the member turns black, as if it were burned by fire,
et porrist aprés la noiror, puis va celle corrosions de membre em membre,	and afterwards the blackness spreads, then goes the corruption of the member to member.
et prent par tout le cors; si te haste dou coper,	And takes hold of the whole body; if you hurry to cover,
et se c’est par la percussion d’aucunes venimouses bestes, si com scorpion de mer et wivre et semblans,	and if it is by the sting of certain poisonous beasts like a sea scorpion or snake and similar,
se li corrosion est au chief dou doi, si le cope, et ne li doner mie espaice de venir jusc’a la main.	If the corruption is at the head of the tooth, strike it, and do not give it any space to come up to the hand.
Et s’elle vient jusc’a la main, si la cope a la jointe, si que la corrosion ne viegne jusc’a bras;	And if it comes up to the wrist, strike it at the joint so that the corruption does not come up to the arm.
et s’elle vient au bras, si le cope au coute; et s’elle passe le coute, c’est li mors,	And if it comes to the elbow, strike at the surface; and if it passes the surface, it is death.
et n’i vaut amenistremens fuers que li quantitez de sa vertut;	and no foreign treatment is effective except for the quantity of its virtue.
et tot ensi fai quant li corrosion vient ou piet: s’elle vient en la premiere jointe, si la cope aprés l’autre jointe;	and thus do as follows when corruption or pus comes: if it comes in the first joint, strike after the next joint.
et s’elle vient ou piet, si cope tout le piet;	If it comes out (or falls) and strikes (it), strike the whole piece.
et s’elle monte en la jambe, si cope a la jointure dou genoil;	If it moves up in the leg, then strike at the knee joint;
et s’elle vient desus le genoil, si n’i a autre engien que dou lassier le malaide a mort;	If it comes above the knee, there is no other remedy for the patient except death.
et li maniere dou coper ou dou soier le membre si est que tu le lie desus et desoz,	The method of striking or treating a limb consists of binding it both above and below;
et estende uns menistres l’un des liiens aval, et uns autres ministres l’autre liien amont,	And stretch one of the ministers (or assistants) the lower limb, and another minister (or assistant) the upper limb.
